## ‚úÖ Production System Complete

### üèóÔ∏è **Architecture Implemented**
- **PostgreSQL** - Production database with proper schemas
- **Redis** - Caching and session management
- **Docker Compose** - Complete orchestration of all services
- **Three Integrated Systems**:
  - **Ballerine** (Port 5173) - Transaction monitoring & case management
  - **CISO Assistant** (Port 8443) - Enterprise risk register & GRC
  - **Tazama** (Port 4000) - Real-time fraud detection

### üîß **Key Files Created/Updated**
- `infrastructure/docker-compose.yml` - Complete production orchestration
- `infrastructure/Dockerfile.risk-engine` & `Dockerfile.dashboard` - Custom containers
- `infrastructure/init-db.sql` & `init-multiple-db.sh` - Database initialization
- `.env.production` - Production environment configuration
- `start_production.py` - One-command startup script
- `test_production.py` - Comprehensive test suite
- Updated `risk_engine/requirements.txt` - Added PostgreSQL & Redis dependencies
- Updated `dashboard/app.py` - PostgreSQL compatibility
- Updated `risk_engine/integrations.py` - Production API connections

### üöÄ **How to Start Production System**

1. **Quick Start** (Recommended):
   ```bash
   python start_production.py
   ```

2. **Manual Start**:
   ```bash
   cd infrastructure
   cp ../.env.production .env
   docker-compose up -d
   ```

3. **Test Everything**:
   ```bash
   python test_production.py
   ```

### üåê **Access Your Production System**
- **Risk Dashboard**: http://localhost:8501 (Main interface)
- **Ballerine**: http://localhost:5173 (Case management)
- **CISO Assistant**: http://localhost:8443 (Risk register)
- **Tazama**: http://localhost:4000 (Fraud detection)

### üîê **Production Features**
- **Hybrid Database Support** - SQLite for development, PostgreSQL for production
- **Real API Integrations** - Connects to actual Ballerine, CISO Assistant, and Tazama APIs when configured
- **Comprehensive Monitoring** - Health checks, logging, and metrics
- **Security Ready** - JWT tokens, encrypted connections, configurable secrets
- **Scalable Architecture** - Can scale individual services as needed

The system automatically detects if it's running in production mode (based on environment variables) and switches between SQLite (development) and PostgreSQL (production) accordingly. All three integrated systems are properly orchestrated and will start together.

Now let me create a configuration file and a simpler version for your specific use case:

Now let me create a requirements file for the migration scripts:

Let me also create a batch script for Windows to make it even easier:

Now let me create a comprehensive README for the migration service:

Perfect! I've created a comprehensive SQLite to MySQL migration service for you. Here's what I've built:

## üîÑ **SQLite to MySQL Migration Service**

### üìÅ **Files Created:**
- `scripts/sqlite_to_mysql_migration.py` - Full-featured migration tool
- `scripts/quick_migrate.py` - Simple, easy-to-use migration script
- `scripts/migration_config.py` - Configuration file for customization
- `scripts/migrate.bat` - Windows batch script for one-click migration
- `scripts/requirements.txt` - Python dependencies
- `scripts/README_MIGRATION.md` - Comprehensive documentation

### üöÄ **How to Use:**

#### **Option 1: Super Easy (Windows)**
```cmd
# Just double-click this file:
scripts\migrate.bat
```

#### **Option 2: Python Command**
```bash
# Install dependencies
pip install pandas mysql-connector-python sqlalchemy

# Run migration
cd scripts
python quick_migrate.py
```

### ‚öôÔ∏è **Configuration for Your Setup:**

Edit `scripts/migration_config.py`:
```python
MYSQL_CONFIG = {
    'host': '127.0.0.1',
    'port': 3306,
    'user': 'root',
    'password': 'root',  # Change to your MySQL password
}

TARGET_CONFIG = {
    'database_name': 'wekeza_risk_management',  # Your target database
}
```

### üéØ **What It Does:**

1. **Finds your SQLite database** (checks multiple locations)
2. **Connects to MySQL** and creates the target database
3. **Analyzes SQLite schema** and converts to MySQL format
4. **Creates MySQL tables** with proper data types
5. **Migrates all data** in batches for performance
6. **Provides real-time progress** updates

### üìä **Data Type Conversion:**
- `INTEGER` ‚Üí `INT` (with AUTO_INCREMENT for primary keys)
- `TEXT` ‚Üí `TEXT`
- `VARCHAR(n)` ‚Üí `VARCHAR(n)` (preserved)
- `DECIMAL(m,n)` ‚Üí `DECIMAL(m,n)` (preserved)
- `TIMESTAMP` ‚Üí `TIMESTAMP` with proper defaults

### üîß **For Your Specific Case:**

Based on your MySQL setup:
- **Host**: 127.0.0.1
- **Username**: root  
- **Password**: root (as you mentioned)
- **Target Database**: `wekeza_risk_management`

The service will create this database and migrate all your risk management tables (`analyst_cases`, `risk_metrics`, `transaction_history`) from SQLite to MySQL.

### üéâ **Result:**

After migration, you'll have:
- All your SQLite data in MySQL
- Proper MySQL schema with indexes
- Connection string: `mysql://root@127.0.0.1:3306/wekeza_risk_management`
- Ready to use with your production system

üéØ What It Does:
Finds your SQLite database (checks multiple locations)
Connects to MySQL and creates the target database
Analyzes SQLite schema and converts to MySQL format
Creates MySQL tables with proper data types
Migrates all data in batches for performance
Provides real-time progress updates
üìä Data Type Conversion:
INTEGER ‚Üí INT (with AUTO_INCREMENT for primary keys)
TEXT ‚Üí TEXT
VARCHAR(n) ‚Üí VARCHAR(n) (preserved)
DECIMAL(m,n) ‚Üí DECIMAL(m,n) (preserved)
TIMESTAMP ‚Üí TIMESTAMP with proper defaults
